< text>
Thai tea fan? Make your way over to L'Moon for their scrumptious soft serve.  This place came up on a Yelp search for ice cream since we were in the area and the good reviews influenced us to stop by. You'll find a small shop with just a counter where you place your order and take it to go. I had perused the menu before arriving and had decided to go with the popular Thai tea soft serve with boba. It was ready in no time and tasted just like a creamy, frozen Thai tea. I had ordered the medium, but should have gone with the small which would have been quite enough. I would certainly return for more of this dessert and it's a good spot to know about as the weather heats up.< /text>

< userid>
112057638330876931618</userid>
< Text>
L'moon Creamery is a unique tea and dessert shop in Upland. You won't find a wide array of different kinds of teas, flavors, and toppings like other places, but rather only a few drinks they specialize in.

The cashier was incredibly friendly. She gave me a sample of their thai tea soft serve, which was rich in taste and creamy. I wasn't looking to get soft serve but I appreciate the gesture. For drinks, she said their best sellers are the thai milk tea, thai tea soft serve float, or the strawberry midori matcha. I asked about the fire rabbit and she said that is another great choice, but it's more like a dessert since it's made of milk, honey boba, cream, and burnt brown sugar on top (no tea).

I decided to get the strawberry midori matcha at 50% sweet. It was a delicious drink and very reminiscent of the strawberry matcha at Boba Guys. However, while I don't like my drinks too sweet, I would say that 50% sweetness wasn't sweet enough. I would recommend getting it at 75% sweetness (if they can do that). The drink also had strawberry chunks instead of just strawberry syrup, which was delicious. Their honey boba was also soft, which I prefer. The price was $4.75, which is about average for most boba places now.

The interior is rather small with only 1 table with 2 chairs and 1 bench. I wouldn't suggest bringing a large group of people to hang out there. But parking was easy with lots of spaces.

They also have a stamp card. After 4 drinks, you get 1 free topping, and after 9 drinks, you get 1 free drink.

Overall, it was a nice place to get specialty drinks and I'll be back to try their other drinks!<//Text>

< Text>
This place is growing on me.  The 1st time I visited, I wasn't a huge fan, but my daughter wanted to try it again, and this time I liked it a lot more.  My favorite menu item is the chocolate chip walnut cookies.  They are AMAZING, especially warmed up!!!  The Thai tea soft serve is unique and very good.  The Thai tea floats are my favorite "drinks".  You can choose vanilla ice cream OR Thai tea soft serve, which they pour Thai tea over and then top with honey boba.  Both are super yummy, but I like the vanilla float slightly more than the soft serve float.  As for the other drinks, I've tried a few of them and disliked every one.  From now on, I will only order the cookies & Thai tea options, and will return often for those!< /Text>

<Gmap_id>0x80c3313f8a031465:0x1739e288fa51a92b<//Gmap_id><text>Rarely do I take a sip of a boba drink and immediately regret that I didn't get a large size. Next time, I'm going for the 24 oz!

It was my first time here since I'm never in this part of town and the owner  (I assume) swiftly handed me some samples, which was a Thai tea, a Thai tea soft serve, and a Thai tea made with almond milk.

I'm not a huge Thai tea fan because I usually think it's too sweet but all these samples were very good! The least sweet was the one made with almond milk.

My love drink is matcha though so I was there for the Strawberry Midori Matcha and with a yelp check-in, I got free honey boba added in.

The drink is beautiful with its triple layered colors but more importantly, is the taste! High-quality matcha with a subtle sweetness from the strawberry jam. Omg! And the boba has to be the softest/chewiest boba I've ever had.

It's a small storefront with one small table and bench seating, so you're not meant to linger, but wow, I'll definitely be back for more!< /text>< date>

<rating>5</rating><text>OK, so I'm giving these folks 5 stars because they are among the very few restaurants in the area, and don't get me wrong - the people running this place are GREAT, and the food is both tasty and safe...  They might only get a 3.5-to-4 star rating if in a more heavily populated area with a higher percentage of the population being familiar to the authentic cuisine.  Just saying.

(If you are from a southern city with lots of great, authentic Mexican options, just get a burger & fries, or go elsewhere and take your chances.)

The burgers are good, the tacos are good - but due to being located in Rio Dell, expectations need to be set realistically.  The locals here are seemingly more interested in a very Americanized version of Mexican cuisine - and The Patron most certainly delivers on this premise.

Their Mexican dishes are extremely Americanized.  If you are looking for truly authentic Mexican food, drive another hour or so north to the Speedy Taco truck in McKinleyville, which is probably the only truly authentic Mexican food within 100+ miles of this very remote North Coast location.  (I left a Google Maps review for them too, take a look if this is what you seek.)

But if you need a good meal and you find yourself here, I can offer some advice.

Either order a burger with fries (above average fries here, btw - and the portion is huge) - or try their tacos or fajitas - or even their appetizer menu, which also tend to be offered in very large portions for appetizers.

Note the prices, their burgers & some other menu items are a bit overpriced, but considering other local options, they are reasonable.

They use an avocado-based green salsa on their street tacos which is VERY mild - if you don't like spicy food, you'll probably LOVE their tacos.  As someone who lived in San Diego and spent a pretty good amount of time in TJ, I can say this: tasty, but very mild and NOT anything like the street food in Mexico.

Their Mexican food is FAR better than any I've tried in Humboldt County, outside of the aforementioned Speedy Taco Truck in McKinleyville, CA, and a couple restaurants in Eureka (La Pechanga & Oaxaca Grill) & Arcata (Carmelita's) which compare in flavor but are far more expensive. DON'T make the mistake of believing that you can get better Mexican food in Fortuna - strange but true - Fortuna has both a large Mexican population, and probably more Mexican restaurants per square mile than any other Humboldt town - but you can't get a decent, or even EDIBLE taco TO SAVE YOUR LIFE.

(If you don't believe me, check out my review (along with photo) of La Costa in Fortuna.  Truly HORRIFIC.)< /text><pics>None</pics><Resp>None<//Resp><GmapID>0x54d46d113abaaaad:0x904d7f38520d878</GmapID></record></dataset><record>

<user_name>Lily Johnson</user_name><Review>First salon haircut after over a year of COVID caution... what a relief.

Positive notes about my experience with Daniela at Salon Bello:

- SCHEDULING: Daniela was able to fit me in for a same-day appointment even though she had been planning to take the day off, which was much appreciated due to my scheduling constraints. It sounds like she's been pretty busy with other people making hair appointments after getting vaccinated.

- COVID MANAGEMENT: Fully vaccinated. Masks on in the salon at all times. Front and back doors kept open for nice air flow. Hand sanitizer readily available. There was one other client in the salon while I was having my hair cut but a good amount of distance was maintained throughout the appointment.

- COMMUNICATION: Appreciated the detailed and individualized consultation on haircut details, styling, products, color options, etc. Daniela spent time to explain why a blunt cut would be a better fit for my hair than layers, and repeatedly checked in about length and how much she was cutting. She was very attentive to the fact that I still wanted to be able to put my hair in a ponytail post-cut.

- ADMIN DETAILS: Scheduling by text is preferred. Payment is accepted by Venmo or cash. Prices are clearly posted in the salon and on the salon's website.

- BONUS DOG POINTS: Daniela's very friendly dog lounges at the front of the salon. She is super cute.

Salon Bello clearly has a lot of devoted fans in the area. Several people walked by the door to say hi and to say how happy they were with their haircuts. I'm glad I was able to get my hair cut with Daniela today and will be back!< /Review><Rating>5<//Rating><GmapID>0x808f7ff948e522ed:0xd48bcf2499b9e645</GmapID>< pictures>

I had to find a new stylist due to the unfortunate current circumstances. My former stylist is a well known color specialist and has become a personal friend but is no longer in the area so finding a new stylist has been an emotional experience.

I noticed a few shops in S.F. that looked interesting. Belo was one of them. It is well located and there are a lot of parking options if you drive. The shop itself has an upbeat mid century vibe without being too cute or too dull Danish Modern. I met the owner Daniela and one of her clients gave her a rave review.

I decided to make an appointment while appointments were possible. She asked me to drop by the shop the day before my appointment for a short chat. I did so. She determined what my expectations were and actually patch tested me to determine if I was allergic to the dye she would be using. I was impressed. She uses a high quality Italian product and I noticed that the surfaces in her shop were sparkling clean. I looked forward to my appointment.

My hair had grown out dry and faded with a lot of grey. We agreed to begin with just getting my hair back to my natural color. Then I could decide about adding the highlights that I wasn‚Äôt quite sure about. I left the shop with silky, shiny dark brown hair that looked totally natural.

I was very pleased and decided to go ahead with highlights. Daniela worked with me to figure out exactly what would work for me. We chose a color and carefully added limited highlights. I lived with my new look for a few days and then I returned, as agreed, to fine tune the results. I asked for a few more highlights around my face, she removed a highlight that did not blend well and we both agreed to darken the highlight color. I left with shiny, silky hair  and highlights that were both slightly edgy and subtle. How do those two things go together? I don‚Äôt know but Daniela pulled it off. She is that rare combination of professionalism and creativity.

Belo Salon is a find! I highly recommend Daniela.<//text>

<rating>5< /rating>< review>
Ordered a combo plate with a side order of falafel, hummus and pita. It's basically a chipotle style Mediterranean place where you pick a base (rice, salad, wrap, pita) then your condiments (hummus, babaghanosh, tabboleh, tatziki, spicy sauce,  garlic sauce, tahini, cucumber, picked peppers, tomatoes, onions, olives, garbanzo, parsley) lastly you pick a protein (falafel, gyro meat, chicken shwarma, and Achilles chicken which is chicken breast cooked on the griddle in its marinade). Combo plate (2 proteins) cost $12.99. side order of falafel (4) was $3.99 and a container of hummus was $3.99 with a pita bread.
We left without our falafel. I called and explained to the owner what had happened and he asked that we come back. He apologized and gave us an extra order of heart shaped falafel.
Everything was delicious, the condiments were so fresh it cuts the heaviness of the dips. The pita is light and fluffy. I wish that our gyro meat and chicken shwarma were freshly carved from the spit, but it was quite busy so they carved some in advance and kept it warm so it dried out a little. Definitely going back.<//review>

~~Parking: Fairly small lot in the front, but there‚Äôs additional parking in the back!

~~Best Part: The Achilles Special!! It was super good! I got Hummus and Achilles spread and everything else on it and it was just a good mash of flavor.

<user>100059040940869232668<//user><name>The Food Goddess</name><Date>1533072724765<//Date><Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
After eating at Achilles 3x and having had the Chicken Schwarma, Chicken Achilles, Falafel and the Beef & Lamb; the Pita sandwiches and the Plate; we are confident in giving them 5 stars. Super friendly service, (on our 1st visit, we explained that we had never been in and the staff couldn't have been more helpful. They even gave us a heart shaped falafel w/their garlic sauce). The Chicken Achilles was super flavorful, the falafel forever changed my idea of what it is supposed to taste like, (soft and tasty inside, crispy on the outside), my bf said the Beef & Lamb was very moist and perfectly seasoned. Unfortunately, the Chicken Schwarma, made with thighs, although very well cooked; was extremely fatty. I didn't remove points though, as they were slammed, had run out of it and had to cook it on the flat top. All of the sides are perfect and their signature sauce is addictive! We'll be back!</Text>

<Text>This is a real gem. I have no idea that the previous kabab place got replaced with this eatery. I went to this place after finding very high ratings and good reviews for this hot new choice. And so glad I am that I made that decision. For quite a while now I was looking for a Mediterranean place for a quick grab which has great food and not overtly expensive. And Achilles is the place.

I and my wife went for the first time on a weekday night around 8 pm. Since it was our first time, the guy at the counter was patient enough to explain us how to go about choosing items and also some suggestions. I chose a chicken shawarma plate and my wife selected an Achilles chicken plate. The base options are rice, salad or half and half of each. Then there are choices of hummus, baba ghanoush and sour cream. There are multiple veggie choices and a bunch of sauces to experiment with. I am pretty sure none of them will turn out bad in any way. The end result is superb and we both liked our plates greatly.

We also tried a side of falafels and that was an order of 4 pieces. They were fried in front of us and given to us within 5 minutes. They taste delicious and fresh - one of the best that I have tasted.

I am definitely coming back for more and I highly recommend to try this place out.</Text><Pics>None</Pics>< response>

< rating>

<review>The falafal is good but nothing else here is worth eating. They have two kinds of gyros rotating on spits but what I ordered wasn't cut fresh from there (like every other restaurant) and was pulled out of a drawer and tasted old and bad.

They have no common drinks (like iced tea) and you end up with a tiny cup of water. The dining area is bombarded with loud music played from a broken radio that stops and starts every 15 seconds. It does this non-stop and none of the employees or management seem to care how annoying it is to hear a song 15 seconds at a time.

Last time I ate here I was sick for the next 5 days. Can't understand why this place is so highly rated when the food, service, and atmosphere is worse than McDonalds</review><Pictures>None< /Pictures><Resp>None</Resp><Gmap_id>0x808fcb8c445d85f5:0x7fbb6a9ea5cf9d2a< /Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
<UserId.>110020188185875708647</UserId.>< text>
The food is really good. I'd talk about the meats, but I couldn't not describe the falafel - a great combination of crunchy/crispy outside and nutty, full flavored interior.

Most important about this place, though, is the people.  The owner is always so pleased to see each customer, and everyone on staff is really happy and helpful. I've seen quite a few people show up with no idea what to try (myself included), and the staff is happy to describe, sample, and give suggestions.

I've found that, more often than not, my enjoyment of food often has more to do with the context of eating it - where you are, the people you are enjoying it with, and the people who make it. The food at Achille's is very tasty on its own and doesn't need any of this to be worth checking out. They do, however, absolutely nail the part about the people who make and serve it. And that's the real reason I keep coming back.<//text>

< review>
My friend and I stopped in to sample the food to see if we wanted Achilles to cater a party for us. We were able to sample schwarma, gyro and falafel--the falafel was so good it was in a class by itself, and heart shaped!--and then their sides, which for us were tabouli, babagnaoush, and hummus. Everything was excellent. We also sampled thier baklava, which is extraordinary. We were so impressed with the food that we hired them to cater our party, which was yesterday, and I got nothing but compliments from our guests. So right now we have some leftovers--yeah!--but in the future I will definitely be going back to enjoy their tasty and satisfying food. Highly recommended. So glad they are in my backyard!</review>

< Text>
Went to the Grand Opening, it was really busy. I got to try their Falafel Pocket, freshly baked Pita bread and wide selection of condiments, my favorite was AMBA (pickled Mango).  It also come with two sides, I had Quinoa Tabouleh (Parsley salad) & Baba Ghanouj (Eggplant salad).   Their prices are very reasonable and you get top notch quality, and very generous portion, overall it is a great value.

I got to also sample the Achilles Garlic spread, goes very well with the Chicken Shawerma, and if you have some room for extra calories, try the Waffle Fries side for $2.99 extra.

Lastly, location is very convenient with easy parking, in a small strip mall about 2 miles from Santana Rowe, off Winchester & Newhall.  There is plenty of seating inside but I like the outdoor patio seating.

Definitely my go to place for fresh Pita, Falafel, and Shawerma.</Text>
